Ni Jianye, the district head of the second district through which the road passes, held a special meeting yesterday to discuss the conscription matters. It was decided to notify the households to be conscripted within five days to remove all obstacles within the route. (3) Only the southern section of the Wuxi-Chengjiang Road is currently open, up to Yanqiao. The northern section from Qingyang to Houteng has also been actively constructed. In addition, the section from Houteng to Nanzha has also been actively started. However, due to the exhaustion of funds, Director Mao previously borrowed 10,000 yuan from the Wuxi-Chengjiang Long-Distance Bus Company. To facilitate the progress of the project, he continued to borrow 5,000 yuan from the company and discussed the northern section project plan and fundraising methods with Li Leng, the County Magistrate of Jiangyin. It was submitted to the County Political Affairs Conference for discussion and decision to implement. It was decided that the entire Wuxi-Chengjiang Road could be opened to traffic within two months.

Ding Shuangsheng Silk Shop to Be Liquidated: Ding Shuangsheng Silk Shop on Da Shi Bridge is in trouble because shop owner Ding Hesheng and his brothers' silk cocoon business failed. This has caused depositors to rush to withdraw their money, leading to disputes. Depositors organized a creditors' group and found that the shop owed a total of 270,000 yuan in deposits, shop funds, customer funds, and collateral. After several meetings, on the 27th of last month, the creditors' group decided that Ding Shuangsheng should pay 20,000 yuan in cash in two installments on April 3rd and 10th, and then discuss future maintenance methods. Feng Xusan, the manager of the silk shop, stated at the scene that he was willing to take full responsibility. On the day before yesterday, when the first installment of 10,000 yuan was due, more than 100 creditors, men and women, gathered at the Chamber of Commerce to wait. At 5:00 PM, Ding Shuangsheng entrusted Ding Yuansheng, Assistant Ye Tongxuan, and Fan Jinwen Rongjianming to attend the meeting and claimed that although 10,000 yuan had been raised, there was no cash available to pay out today and requested an extension. The creditors believed that this was a deliberate delay and could not agree to it. It was impossible to maintain the status quo. They immediately obtained permission from the County Chamber of Commerce to seal up the goods in the shop that evening, together with the Silk and Cloth Trade Association and the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday morning, it was decided at the Chamber of Commerce to allow the inventory of the shop to be checked today (the 5th) and liquidated. It was also decided to hire a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the court, requesting the seizure of the assets of Ding and manager Feng Xusan to pay off the debts.

Opium Trafficker Arrested and Sent to Court for Trial: A man from Anhui named Sun Lianxi has been engaged in opium trafficking for a long time. He has never been caught because of his cunning methods. At 6:00 PM the day before yesterday, Sun carried a large amount of opium and arrived in Wuxi by train from Beijing, intending to sell it in the countryside. After getting off the train, he looked flustered and walked straight towards Zhou Shanbang. He was spotted by Fan Jinying, a railway police officer at the station, who suspected the passenger's behavior. He immediately went forward to search and found six packages of Sichuan opium (weighing ten pounds in total) in his rattan basket. He took the man and the evidence to the stationmaster's office. Yesterday, Ma Jirui, the head of the police section, prepared a document and sent him to the county court for trial.

Changshu 93

Petition of Sandbar Residents Concerning River Dredging: In this county's Nansha District, the Sanzhangpu One, Two, Three, and Four Wo Rivers were jointly planned by Changshu and Taicang counties in the 13th year of the Republic of China, and it was decided to dredge them in sequence. The One, Two, and Three trunk rivers have already been completed, but the Four trunk river has not yet started construction. The farmers in the district believe that the Four trunk river is the lifeline of the entire water conservancy system. Although the One, Two, and Three trunk rivers provide drainage, the Four trunk river is necessary for the regional relationship. Chen Qiwei, the former director of the Construction Bureau, went to the province to meet with Sun, the director of the Construction Department, to request approval for the dredging of the Four trunk river, but Director Sun did not approve it due to a lack of funds. Now, 100,000 mu of farmland in the sandbar is about to become barren due to the lack of water conservancy. Therefore, the farmers in the district organized a large-scale petition meeting, electing more than 80 representatives to go to the city on the 1st to petition the Party and government organs for the dredging of the Fourth trunk river to benefit water conservancy. They first went to the county government, but the county magistrate had returned to his hometown, so Jin Minjun, the head of the First Section, received them and promised to report their intentions to the county magistrate in the future. Later, they went to the Construction Bureau and the County Party Branch to petition. It is reported that the representatives will go to the provincial government to petition again if the petition in the county is ineffective.

Nantong 94

Maritime Pacification to Be Completed by Deadline: The Provincial Government's Pacification Supervisory Office, believing that the coastal area of northern Jiangsu is not peaceful, jointly convened the Navy Department to conduct a large-scale investigation and handling. A temporary office was established in Tongcheng. Zhang Han, the director of the Wusong Water Police District, also led police ships and patrol boats to Tongzhou to suppress bandits in the Lvsi area. This maritime pacification operation is scheduled to be completed before Qingming Festival in order to benefit the fishing boats on Guyu Wangfan.

Sand Field Case: The Provincial Government ordered the county government to confiscate 1,100 mu of illegally collected shoal land in the Liu Hai Sand Jisheng case and return it to the state. County Magistrate Zhang sent police to arrest the main culprits in the case, Wu Xingchi and Zhang Hongxiang, and ordered them to pay the shoal land. At the same time, the Education Bureau accused Wu and Zhang of endangering educational property. Wu and others then requested to be transferred to the court. The county government submitted a report to the province for approval. On the 3rd, instructions were received that since the county had already arrested Wu Xingchi and Zhang Hongxiang, the administrative part of the case should be expedited and concluded separately. The cases of Wu Xingchi and others burning warehouses and robbing beans will be investigated and transferred to the judicial organs for handling after the main case is executed, in order to avoid taking the lighter road.

Jiangyin 95

Chengwu Steamship Still Difficult to Operate: The Chengwu steamship has been suspended for several days since the villagers of Wucheng counties prevented its operation. Passengers are quite inconvenient. On the 2nd, Xinhua Company sent Tan Yansheng to Chengjiang to petition the county government to consult with Wujin County to detain the leading villagers who caused the trouble and to ask the water police to send patrol boats to protect it in order to open the ship. But it is reported that certain villagers such as villagers in Shichuang and other places at the intersection of Chengjiang and Wuxi invited villagers to a meeting at a certain place the day before yesterday, intending to deal with Chengxi small ferries by extraordinary means. The small ferry company is planning to deal with the way.

Police Team Captures Bandits and Sends Them to County for Trial: Ma Huaizhong, captain of the fourth squadron of police stationed at Wangjiadai and commander of the guerrilla team, received a report the day before yesterday from Zuo Guilin, instructor of the Sanjia Qiu Security Corps, that Yao Shengrong's home in Xiyanwei, Wushan, had been repeatedly blackmailed for silver by red bandits. Ma Captain heard the report and led the team to find the Red bandit He Genbao, and Yao Jintang, the son of the victim Yao Shengle, and cotton robes, shirts, flashlights, etc. at Yao's home. The team sent everything to the county for trial on the 2nd.

Yangzhou 96

Extortionist Caught in Trap: Li Zongxin, who lives in Changgeng Lane, Genzi Street, in this city, used to work as a clerk in Yangzhou Customs. Since the customs was abolished, he has been living in leisure. Because he is often sick, his wife, Jiang, manages all the affairs in the family. On the twenty-fifth day of the lunar new year, the family's fur coats and other items were stolen. Because her husband was ill, the woman did not report the case. Recently, she learned that the surname Li had received three letters from bandits demanding 300 yuan. Yesterday (the 2nd), another letter came, ordering the money to be wrapped in newspapers and delivered to the land temple at the entrance of the alley. Jiang reported to the third police station under the jurisdiction, and Xu Patrol Officer designed a package in the same way, tied with linen rope, and fastened a copper bell to the linen rope. Four plainclothes policemen ambushed around the alley. At the appointed time, an old man named Li Dengxing came to the temple, took the newspaper package, and the police heard the bell sound of the paper bag and went forward to arrest him. Just out of the alley, a young man named Li Shanzhi, the owner of Li Rongsheng Paint Shop near the alley, went to the police and claimed that the person you arrested was his father and asked to be released immediately. Patrol Officer Xu believed that Li's father was highly suspicious and should not be released without authorization. He took Li Shanzhi with him for interrogation. Li's father and son both denied the matter. The patrol officer then ordered Li Dengxing to write numbers, which resembled the handwriting in the threatening letter. Then Li's father and son were sent to the first bureau for disposal. It is reported that Chen Peiqiu from Dai Chunlin Incense Powder Shop in Gengzi Street and other nine families submitted a request to the first bureau for guarantee. The first bureau considered the case to be serious and transferred Li and the guarantee to the general bureau for verification.

Gaoyou 97

Fushengchang Tobacco Shop Suffers Fire: Fushengchang Tobacco Shop in Zhongshikou, this city, caught fire at about 4:00 AM this morning (the 2nd) due to carelessness. The fire light illuminated the sky for a while. Fortunately, the fire dragons of the shops were effectively extinguished, and it did not affect other shops. However, the buildings of Fushengchang were completely destroyed. It is said that the losses were huge.

Bandits Rob and Injure People in Qiujiazhuang: More than ten bandits suddenly came to Qiujiazhuang in the eastern countryside of the county last night, each reporting guns and weapons, and swarmed up the village. Farmer Qiu Yongkuan rang the gong and shouted to catch the thieves. When the bandits heard the gong, they opened fire and shot, injuring Qiu Yongkuan, Qiu Minglian, and Qiu Sun, three men and women, on the spot. Then they robbed several families, with losses estimated at about three or four hundred yuan.

Jiaxing 98

Jealousy Almost Leads to Murder: The wife of Yuan Laoren, a Wenzhou overseas Chinese in Jiaxing Jiaolidi Street, had an affair with her husband's nephew, Yuan Enpei, in her hometown of Wenzhou. After immigrating to Jiaxing, the aunt and nephew both built thatched houses on both sides of the river in Jiaolidi Street and rented land for planting to make a living. Her husband worked as a servant in Fengqiao village. Recently, the wife had a secret affair with her neighbor, Ye Hecan, which was discovered by Enpei. The night before last, he secretly went to his aunt's thatched house and entered the bedroom, but he did not find anyone and returned. The next night, the wife, believing that Enpei was of a lower status and should not interfere improperly, gathered Ye Hecan, Ye Heshang, Li Amao, and others, each holding weapons, and led them to twist and beat Enpei, causing him to be covered in bruises and unconscious. After someone reported to the Guanyinge police station, they sent police to take Enpei to the court for examination and then to Fuyin Hospital for treatment. At the same time, the wife and Ye Hecan were arrested. After interrogation by the court, they were ordered to be imprisoned. Enpei's injuries will be determined before further punishment is ordered.

Ningbo 99

Large Number of Bandits Arrested: According to a telegram from the Liu Du Security Corps, the Zhenhai Zhuangshi Public Security Bureau said that it found more than ten people with suspicious behavior at about 4:00 pm on March 31, please send police to come and catch them with it. After receiving the telegram, He Jisheng, director of the bureau, led patrol captain Zhou Mengxiong and five policemen to the area and there were indeed many people with suspicious behavior gathering in a temple. The director of the bureau immediately cooperated with the security and turned to catch the suspected persons, and arrested Yu A'quan, Wang Quanyou, Ye Hongfu, Gao Laohu, Lu A'xiang, Wang Xiaojiang, Chen Shijin, Wang A'da and other eight people on the spot and seized three white-langlin handguns, 29 bullets. They were immediately sent to the county government for interrogation. The bandits confessed that they had just arrived from Shanghai and wanted to kidnap Fang Moumou, a wealthy Lian family in Koushu, because the gate was tightly closed and there was no way to start, so they planned to go to another place, which led to their capture.

Huzhou 100

Security Corps Rescues Three Hostages: According to reports, bandits were frequenting the area near Hongxingqiao in the Huzhou district. The Yinjia Village Security Corps organized a party and many soldiers and armed them and went to search door-to-door, and found three hostages, Feng Zhongxin, etc., in a thatched shed of a certain surname, while the bandits had long since fled. Educational News Highlights

Education Survey on Secondary Education Conditions 101

The Ministry of Education has reissued survey forms and issued a circular to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities to investigate the status of secondary education across the country. The Ministry of Education issued a survey form last year to investigate the status of secondary education across the country. The form was to be reported by the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities. The Ministry of Education also issued a telegram this year urging that it be expedited, but the departments and bureaus have not fully complied with the reporting requirements, and the names and numbers of public and private secondary schools across the country need to be verified. Therefore, it is not appropriate to delay any longer. The Ministry of Education has specially issued a simple survey form for public and private secondary schools in each province and city, asking the department to fill it out and send it to the Ministry within one week of receiving the document for preliminary calculation. Those who have not reported the 18-year secondary school survey statistics form or have not fully reported them should still expedite the reporting. This is extremely important, and it is hereby ordered.

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Approves Jiangyin's 19-Year Work Plan 102

Lu Lifan, Director of the Jiangyin Education Bureau, previously drafted a 19-year work plan and submitted it to the Department of Education for approval. The instructions from the Department are recorded below. (1) In addition to the county high school, there are public Nanshan and private Zhengcun in the urban area, and private Qingyang Yangshe Changjing three schools in the rural area. Graduates of primary schools in the county, both in the city and in the countryside, do not have to worry about not having a place to study. At this time, the funding for universal education is extremely scarce, and the county-level junior high school should indeed expand, and private high schools do not need subsidies. (2) Although senior grades in primary schools are needed, the county's education funds are insufficient for universal education, so additional grades cannot be added arbitrarily before additional funding can be raised to prevent abuses. (3) The academic performance of the special students recruited by the rural teachers' colleges is very poor and is accepted for accomodation. Recruitment should be stopped this year, and if teachers are needed, a one-year normal school should be opened to recruit junior high school graduates. (4) Since the county already has a practical elementary school and a rural teacher practical elementary school, they should be closed. (5) The name of the district representative should be abolished immediately. Those with good results should be changed to district-run, and those who are not well-run should be closed immediately. (6) The creation of the Party Boy Scout cause belongs to the scope of universal education and shall not use social education or voluntary funds.

Zhejiang University's Funding Still Allocated from Zhejiang Province's Business Tax 103

The funding for National Zhejiang University has been missing since January of this year, and the university's difficult situation has been reported in the newspapers. It is now known that the university received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance yesterday stating that it had agreed with the Ministry of Education that the university's final expenses would still be fully allocated from Zhejiang Province's business tax. Before the business tax is levied, the ministry will allocate 30,000 yuan per month starting in March, and the province will raise the remaining amount. The original telegram from the Ministry of Finance is recorded below: National Zhejiang University, Jian Yang telegram received. The funding for your school has been agreed with the Ministry of Education that the ministry will allocate 30,000 yuan per month starting in March, and the province will raise the remaining amount. Once Zhejiang Province's business tax is levied, it will be fully allocated from the business tax. In addition to having issued separate orders to the Ministry of Education and the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance, I hope you will check and handle it. Ministry of Finance, Dong.

Local

Private Universities in Shanghai That Have Been Registered Petition for Allocation of Funds for Subsidies 106

Letter to the Ministry of Education

Private universities in Shanghai that have been registered have petitioned the Ministry of Education for an allocation of funds for subsidies due to the need to increase school affairs and the economic difficulties. The original petition is recorded below:

To the Ministry of Education for funding shortages and requesting allocation of funds for subsidies. All of our schools were founded by private individuals and have been funded by student tuition fees and donations from people in society over the years. We have worked hard to manage and the scale is rough. Since being registered by the Ministry, school affairs have become more developed, and the number of students has increased daily. However, in accordance with the requirements of the Ministry, the needs have also expanded daily. School buildings urgently need to be added and equipment urgently needs to be enriched. We are trying to support ourselves by patching things up, and the difficult situation has long been understood. Now that construction is in full swing, there is an urgent need for talent, and the number of national universities is not large, so young people who want to study have the concern of being left out. In the Party and the country, the authorities also feel the sigh of the difficulty of talent. Our schools cultivate specialized talents and research advanced academics. Our operations are no different from national universities, and the service of graduates to society is obvious. It is also no less than that of national universities. The funding for national universities is often hundreds of thousands to millions each year, while private universities have no help at all. The same education institutions, bearing the same responsibility for cultivating specialized talents, the treatment of the lush and withered is so different. How can this be called fair when we consider the principles of education? Last year, the Second National Education Conference passed the third article of the program for improving higher education. The first item stated that "Private universities, colleges, and specialized schools that have been registered and have excellent academic performance may be subsidized by the central or provincial government, or by the Ministry of Education in consultation with the Gengkuan Education Fund Committee." The eleventh item of the tenth article stipulated that "Starting from the 19th year, the central government should increase funding" and that "Subsidize 300,000 yuan for the expenses of registered private universities and specialized schools." The current economic situation of the schools is in urgent need of subsidies. We hereby jointly petition the Ministry to take the supreme intention of improving higher education and implement the plan of the previous National Education Conference, and quickly transfer it to the central government for allocation of funds for subsidies or transfer it to the Gengkuan Education Fund Committee for allocation of subsidies so that our schools can develop step by step according to the planned plan, then it is not just the good fortune of our schools, but the future of the Party and the country. Sincerely presented to the Minister of Education, Jiang.

Annual Meeting of the British Boy Scouts Association 108

—Held Today at the Merrimington Ground—

China Team Decides to Participate with the 64th Regiment

City Scout Council Decides to Extend Term for Reorganization

The annual competition of the Boy Scouts Association initiated by the British Boy Scouts Association in this city has always attracted enthusiastic participation. This year, it will be held at the Merrimington Ground on Hongqiao Road at 6:30 PM on April 6th. Participants include teams from seven countries, with the Chinese team deciding to participate with the 64th Regiment and senior Boy Scouts. The City Boy Scout Council, to foster friendship among international Boy Scouts, has specially prepared a large silver shield to award to the winning international Boy Scout team. However, this silver shield is only allowed to be retained by the winning team for one year. If the team wins for three consecutive years, it will be permanently retained by that winning team.

Furthermore, since its establishment, the City Boy Scout Council will reach its term in June. According to Article 2 of the Organizational Regulations of the Special City Council of the Chinese Boy Scouts, it should have completed its term and held elections for the second council. However, as it is the middle of the school term and various group activities are in full swing, an immediate election would have a significant impact on the Boy Scout movement in this city. It is reported that the council has obtained approval from the Chinese Boy Scout Headquarters to hold the council election at the end of July.

Guanlan Experimental School to be Established at Xu Gong Bridge 109

The various facilities of the rural improvement experimental area established by the China Vocational Education Society at Xu Gong Bridge in Kunshan have attracted considerable attention from various parties. Japanese Law Graduate Shen Jiong Returns to China 110

Mr. Shen Jiong, courtesy name Jiu Gao, is from Jiangsu Province. He studied in the Department of Politics and Economics at St. John's University, and later went to Japan for further study. In the spring of the sixteenth year, he entered the Faculty of Law at Waseda University, specializing in law. He graduated this spring with honors and was awarded a Bachelor of Laws degree by the Japanese government. It is noted that Mr. Shen is the first Chinese student to receive a Bachelor of Laws degree from Waseda University. In addition to his dedication to law, Mr. Shen has also actively engaged in social work. During his four years in Japan, he served as chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Association of Chinese Students in Japan, chairman of the Waseda University Student Association, chairman of the Sino-Japanese Friendship Association, and secretary of the Sino-Indian Friendship Association. Chinese scholars in Japan have unanimously praised him, and the Japanese also deeply admire him. Now that he has completed his studies and returned to China, it is expected that he will make great contributions to Chinese culture. Mr. Shen has been appointed by Mr. Li Peitian, president of the Shanghai Cultural College, to manage school affairs and serve as the director of Maritime Law. Officials in Beijing have also repeatedly sent letters inviting him to Beijing for consultations.

Seibu Wins the Scott Cup Again 113

—Yesterday's Victory over Scoder with a Score of Two to One

Yesterday, the Seibu football team defeated the Scoder team with a score of two to one at the Shen Garden, winning the Scott Cup. From now on, the three major championships of the Seibu Football Club's A-League competition, the Senior Cup and the Scott Cup, are all in the team's possession. They should be high-spirited and excited.

Seibu Team:

Weijinsheng

Scott: Helei, Toner

Blatt, Gaxu, Faras

Gibson, Huisihua, Jack

Yaklai

Scoder:

Dulai

Jemusi, HeleiDe, Hamildun

Marseis, Duge, Blatt

Gelaite, Nair, Simisi

Queerden

The Hero's Head Turns Out to be Extraordinary

At the beginning of the fierce battle, the Scoder team took the lead, but Seibu defended effectively, and a stalemate ensued. After thirty minutes, both sides' goals remained unscathed. At this time, the military goalkeeper Marseis caught the ball and kicked it forward fiercely. Seibu's general, center forward Farlas, with the ambition of "not entering the tiger's den, how can one obtain the tiger cubs," single-handedly attacked. The ball hit his head with a thud and rebounded into the net, achieving the first great success. The audience, half of whom were cheering for Seibu, responded with a great cheer.

Yellow-Haired Divine Foot Achieves a Surprise Victory

Weijinsheng, the famous left-winger on the sea, is also the reason why Seibu's forwards are more elite than other teams. Not three minutes after Seibu won the first goal, this famous left-winger dribbled the ball from the side to the center and shot towards the goal within five steps. The Scoder goalkeeper punched it out with one arm, fortunately without incident. After another seven minutes, Weijinsheng revisited the scene, and his divine leg swept across and succeeded, creating a 2-0 lead in the first half.

Dulai's Header Makes the Whole Field Pale

At the start of the second half, Scoder's center forward Blatt injured his left foot and switched positions with right-winger Queerden. The spectators thought that the military's momentum would decline due to the injury of a major general. Unexpectedly, Scoder stood their ground with their backs to the water and their spirits were high. Seibu was instead trapped by them. Within ten steps of the goal, the Scoder army repeatedly shot, but because of aiming without targets, it was difficult to achieve results. In the last ten minutes, the Scoder army's midfielder made a very good pass, and the landing point was next to the goal. The left-winger Dulai headed the ball in, and the ball broke into the net. Scoder regained a goal and hope was born. Seeing the situation was not good, Seibu tried their best to defend, and finally won the Scoder team with a score of 2-1, winning the Scoto Cup. The referee was Li Nuosi, and the line judges were Le Xiurong and Fan Ensi.

The Huazhong Football Team, Participating in the Regional Competition for the First Time, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 116

Team Leader Song Ruhai Arrives in Shanghai Today - A Total of Twenty-Three Team Members

—The North China Team is Expected to Arrive in Shanghai Tonight—

The National Regional Football Competition will be held in Shanghai soon. Except for the South China team, which did not come due to unforeseen circumstances, the North China and Central China teams have participated to support the grand event. According to a reporter, this is the first time that the Huazhong football team has participated in the regional competition, opening a record in the history of Chinese sports. The team, led by Song Ruhai, has a total of twenty-three members and arrived in Shanghai yesterday. They are staying at the Yizhong Apartment on Pupo Road. Mr. Song will only be able to arrive here by plane today due to other matters. The reporter met with Mr. Zhou Qingxuan and Secretary Zhao Lanquan of the team yesterday, and their conversation is summarized as follows:

The Recent Situation of Sports in Central China

Sports in Central China, especially in Hunan, used to be very developed. However, since the communists occupied Changsha, the schools have been burned down, education has been greatly impacted, and sports have also disappeared.

Recovery has been quite difficult. Jiangxi Province is still trapped in communist difficulties. Sichuan Province has little access due to transportation issues. Therefore, Wuhan should be the center. Wuhan University is still in its early stages and is still developing. Although Hankou's sports are very immature, the YMCA and the Hankou Sports Association have made great achievements in promoting them. Basketball and football teams have sprung up. The YMCA team has the strongest strength in basketball, and the Sanyu and Municipal Government teams in football. However, due to economic exhaustion and the lack of suitable venues, development has been slow.

Liu Wendao Enthusiastically Promotes Sports

This time, the Huazhong football team is traveling east. Economic difficulties are extremely difficult. The estimated cost is more than 1,000 yuan. At first, only more than 400 yuan was raised. Liu Wendao, the mayor of Hankou, generously donated 300 yuan to promote sports, showing great enthusiasm. Furthermore, there is no suitable football field in Hankou. Only a wasteland in the park is used to compete with Westerners. It is necessary to go to the Western Merchants Racecourse to receive their hospitality, which is truly embarrassing. The Municipal Government has passed a resolution to raise 900,000 yuan to build a large-scale sports field, which will be completed before September. The 5th Huazhong Games will be held here. Mr. Liu is actively preparing. In the future, the promotion of sports in Central China will rely on Mr. Liu's promotion.

Motivation for Participating in the Regional Competition

Mr. Song Ruhai spares no effort in promoting sports. He currently works at the Hankou YMCA, and the YMCA basketball team was trained by him. Mr. Song, seeing the lack of vitality in sports in Central China, worked hard to advocate the organization of a football team to participate in the National Regional Competition. After various difficulties, the representative team was finally produced. The purpose of this trip is to connect with all parties and arouse interest in sports in Central China. Knowing that the skills are inferior to others, victory or defeat is not the goal.

Representatives and Origin of Funding

Most of the Huazhong representative team was selected from the Hankou Municipal Government and the Sanyu Sports Association football teams. A football match was held with Tongwen in Jiujiang. Tongwen won the Huazhong Football Championship last year with a score of 1-0, but this year they lost to the Hankou team with a score of 1-2. In the end, it was decided that Hankou would represent the team. A telegram was sent to Tongwen to invite them to participate, but it is regrettable that the selected team members did not come. The funding was donated by the Municipal Government football team for 346 yuan, and Mayor Liu donated 300 yuan. There is still a large shortfall. Currently, Shen Siliang of the National Sports Association has agreed to make every effort to find a solution.

Huazhong Football Team Lineup

In addition to participating in the regional competition, the team will have several friendly matches. The team leader is Song Ruhai, the staff are Sun Honglie and Tang Xingtian, the secretary is Zhao Lanquan, and the lineup is as follows:

Municipal Fishery Promotion Conference Held 119

First Day Record

The municipal fishery improvement promotion conference was inaugurated yesterday (the 4th) morning, with an attendance of no less than three thousand people, causing the auditorium (at the Minli Middle School Alliance) to be unusually crowded. Central representatives Yang Qingyuan, Mayor Zhang Yuejun, Minister of Industry Kong Xiangxi (represented by Han Yougang), Ministry of Industry representatives Zou Bingwen and Li Dongxiang, City Party Committee Standing Committee member Wu Bokang, Jiangsu Agricultural and Mining Director He Yushu, City Social Affairs Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan, and others all arrived on time. Mayor Zhang presided over the meeting, with the conference's Deputy Secretary-General Zhou Hanmei and Chief Editor Zhou Jianyin recording the proceedings. The meeting commenced with the chairman's opening address (full text below), followed by speeches from central representatives and various organizations. Director He then delivered a reply speech. After the conference secretary-general reported on the preparations, a group photo was taken, and the meeting adjourned. The conference then hosted a tour of the exhibition. At 2:00 PM, entertainment was held, including (1) a fishery film, (2) music by the Xinhua Art College, and (3) song and dance performances by the Sisters' Song and Dance Troupe. Over 5,600 people attended the conference and exhibition in succession, making it an unprecedented grand event in the fishery industry. The speeches are recorded below:

Mayor's Opening Remarks

The purpose of today's meeting is to conduct a grand promotion for China's coastal fishery. The decline of China's fishery did not begin today. Examining the reasons for its failure, half are due to foreign aggression, and half are due to our own lack of self-improvement. According to international law, all countries' fishing boats have freedom on the high seas, except within three nautical miles of the coast, which is reserved exclusively for the use of fishermen of the sovereign state. Foreign fishing is not allowed to intrude. Now, there are no less than sixty or seventy foreign vessels fishing in the waters off Jiangsu and Zhejiang in China. They started by using Taiwan as a base to invade the fisheries of our southern coastal provinces. Then, they used Qingdao and Dalian as bases to invade the fisheries of our northern coastal provinces. Recently, they want to use Shanghai as a base to invade the fisheries of our central coastal provinces. If we do not improve in time, our entire coastal fishery will fall into the hands of foreigners, and the livelihoods of our millions of coastal fishing households will be cut off. If the source of Chinese fish is cut off, then all the people in the country who eat fish will have to rely on foreign fish. This will not only add to the hundreds of millions of dollars in losses each year but also inflict a major blow on the super-national economy due to fish imports. And those who suffer will not only be a mere few million fishing households. Furthermore, the failure of our country's fishery lies in the lack of self-improvement of our country's fishermen. Today's world is a scientific world, and competition in industry and commerce is also nothing more than scientific competition. Therefore, the success or failure of competition always depends on the degree of scientific progress. The reliance of fisheries on science is no less than that of agriculture and mining. When the winds are treacherous, and the tides are irregular, we rely on meteorology; to operate boats and use nets, we rely on mechanics; to identify species and observe their movements, we rely on aquatic science. In addition, skillful storage and efficient marketing, all the techniques of industrial and commercial competition, are applicable to fishery, and the degree of danger in fishery is ten to a hundred times greater than in other industries and commerce. Now, our country's fishing industry clings to old ways, does not seek progress, or is content with fate, or is an accomplice to others. It is only a matter of time before our entire fishery is ruined. Now, this conference makes a loud and urgent appeal, saying: Fishery is the lifeline of our millions of fishing households, and it concerns the economy of our four hundred million compatriots. If we do not fight for it, we will never have a chance to rise again. The way to remedy this, in terms of fishery, is to feel the weight of responsibility and strive for improvement. In terms of society, we should know that fishery is related to the people's livelihood, and we should find ways to advocate for it so that talent and capital gradually gather. And the most important thing is that the national populace should support the government's diplomatic policy and eliminate all foreign aggression. Only then can our country's industry and commerce compete with the large industries and large businesses of the East and West. (Omitted below)

Central Party Department Representative's Admonition

Central representative Yang Qingyuan delivered an admonitory speech, saying: Today, the Jiangsu Province and Shanghai Municipality Fishery Improvement Promotion Conference is holding its opening ceremony here. I am very pleased to be here to participate on behalf of the Central Government. Among the production industries, fishery is a very important one. In primitive society, when people's knowledge was not advanced, they already knew how to fish. In the development history of various ethnic groups, there was a period of fishery society. In our country, nets were invented during the time of Fu Xi, more than four thousand years ago. Our country also has tens of thousands of miles of coastline. Based on this, fishery in our country should have long-term progress, and the amount of production should rank first in the world. But the facts tell me that our country's fishery has not only not progressed but is also declining day by day. Those engaged in fishery are either stagnant and complacent or become bandits. The reasons for this are: first, fishermen have immature knowledge and do not know how to apply scientific methods; second, the active aggression and destruction by imperialists. Countries such as England, Japan, America, and Russia apply scientific methods, strive to improve fishing gear, and constantly research. The government protects the fishery and makes every effort to reward it. Therefore, countries such as England, Japan, America, and Russia now produce several times more each year than our country. Even our country's markets are filled with foreign salted fish and fresh fish. If this continues and no remedy is found, not only will our millions of fishermen be at the end of their ropes, but the economic problems of the entire country will also be greatly affected, falling into an unmanageable situation. The Jiangsu and Shanghai party and government authorities, in view of this dangerous situation, initiated the organization of a fishery improvement promotion conference to display the fishery of this country and the fishery conditions of European and American countries in one hall, to awaken the Chinese people and to serve as a basis for research and progress. I hope that the representatives present will visit and then do their best to publicize it. It must be known that the improvement of fishery is not only the active reward and passive protection of the government, but also the efforts of the people to improve themselves in order to seek the improvement of health, the rapid progress of business, and the increase of production. In the future, efforts should be made in both economic talent and personnel. Then, the crisis of Chinese fishery can be easily resolved. I put forward this point, hoping that everyone will work hard to complete it.

Minister of Industry Kong Xiangxi's Speech

Jiangsu is the most important place for fishery in the Southeast. Taking the Shengshan fishing port as an example, fishing boats from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Fujian provinces gather there, numbering no less than several thousand. Other ports such as Lvsi and Xinyang are also abundant in marine products and densely populated with fishing boats. Therefore, the Premier's industrial plan includes the provision to construct fishery ports in various ports. Shanghai is China's only major trading port. The annual sales of domestic salted and fresh fish, combined with the output of foreign seas and rivers, are about 20 million yuan, while the sales and transit of foreign marine products are nearly 50 million yuan each year. Therefore, Shanghai is indeed a large market for marine products. The Jiangsu Provincial Party Affairs Consolidation Committee, the Agricultural and Mining Department, the Shanghai Municipal Party Committee, the Municipal Government, and the Jiangsu Provincial Fishery Experiment Station, in view of the importance of aquatic products in Jiangsu's position and the breadth of their sales, and deeply regretting that people in society are indifferent and do not pay much attention to this enterprise, have jointly organized a fishery improvement promotion conference. New fishing methods, books, and specimen displays are placed in the venue for people to visit, in order to promote social attention to fishery and to induce their entrepreneurial spirit. I very much approve of this. This department, as the highest competent authority for fishery administration, is well aware of the plight of coastal fishermen. Therefore, since its establishment, although only four months have passed, in terms of the passive aspect, it has already requested the State Council to pass the exemption of fish tax and fishery tax, in order to relieve the suffering of fishermen over the years. As for the active aspect, all aspects of promotion, protection, improvement, and crackdown are being carried out with all efforts and without any slackening. There are four points that can be reported to you: (1) Regarding promotion, such as the plan for ocean-going fishery incentive funds, is in fact due to the lack of entrepreneurial concepts in our country's fishery industry and the lack of attention to ocean-going fishery. Therefore, 250,000 yuan has been included in the national budget for the 20th year as ocean-going fishery incentive funds, and it is also planned to consult with the seven coastal provinces to also propose a corresponding bonus in the provincial budget to encourage newly built ocean-going fishing vessels to seek to initiate and guide the sound of ocean-going fishery. (2) Regarding protection, it is planned to establish four special management agencies for fishery protection in the seven coastal provinces, to purchase general-purpose ships to specifically prevent pirates and protect the safety of fishery. (3) Regarding improvement, fishery is different from various mechanical industries because marine conditions and climate are related to the growth of fish and their habitats also vary. Therefore, the fishing gear that is suitable for Country A may not be applicable to Country B. Therefore, the excellence of a country's fish catching, manufacturing, and aquaculture technologies relies on rich experience, and the acquisition of experience relies on experimentation. This department plans to include 500,000 yuan in the national budget for the 20th year to plan the establishment of a central model aquatic product experiment station to engage in experimental fishing, manufacturing, and aquaculture courses, and to set up two departments for publicity and lectures to transmit the results of experiments to fishermen so that those who operate in aquatic products have something to learn from. (4) Regarding crackdown, in recent years, foreign fishing boats have invaded, and everyone has known what the newspapers have reported. This department pays special attention to this, and has repeatedly discussed the crackdown methods at the State Council meeting and consulted with relevant parties. Now, a part of it has been resolved, and there are still those who should be dealt with through negotiation. In addition to always consulting with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to proceed, the overall goal is to achieve a satisfactory resolution. In short, the construction of national undertakings requires the cooperation of the people and the government to be effective. Now, the decline of our country's fishery has reached its extreme. All the ends that should be prospered and reformed are numerous. However, if our people can be united from top to bottom and strive forward, then the already declining fishery can be restored in the shortest time, and the holding of this meeting today is not only not in vain, but will also greatly contribute to the improvement of our coastal fishery. This is what this department encourages itself, and it should also be what we encourage each other.

Social Affairs Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan's Speech

City Social Affairs Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan delivered a speech, briefly stating that when we look at the depression of China's coastal fishery on the one hand, and the urgency of foreign fishing invasion on the other hand, we know that holding this improvement promotion conference today is really an urgent matter. At the same time, we know that if we want to seek the improvement of fishery, we must first pay attention to the consumption aspect of fishery, because fish are most easily corrupted. If consumption is not promoted, even if production increases, as a result of not being able to sell, they will only be sold at the lowest price, or even rot and be discarded. For example, all the fishing boats in Shanghai last year were greatly affected because Japanese fish were sold in large quantities in this city, resulting in low fish prices and unsustainable business. If Chinese fishery suddenly increases in production, and new fishing boats suddenly increase several times or dozens of times, I believe that the result will still tend to fail. Therefore, while we want to develop Jiangsu's fishery, it is especially necessary to plan the construction of the sales and consumption business in Shanghai, because Shanghai is the concentration of fishery in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, and it is also one of the international markets. The reason why this conference is not held in the production area but in Shanghai is for this reason, etc.

Agricultural and Mining Department Director He Yushu's Reply Speech

China's coastal fishery has declined to the extreme. If we do not seek improvement, our millions of coastal fishermen will be finished. Finishing off millions of fishermen is the end of the matter. However, the forces of imperialism take the opportunity to invade, which not only finishes off the livelihoods of our millions of fishermen but also endangers the entire Chinese nation. Now, the Soviet Province and the Municipal Association have jointly organized this improvement promotion conference. Although they do not dare to say that there are any achievements, this play must be done. At the beginning of today's meeting, all sectors of society participated enthusiastically, which shows that society already has a considerable understanding of fishery. I hope that the people and the government will jointly do this play to promote and improve fishery in the future.

China Child Welfare Association Promotes Children's Day (Continued) 120

Detailed Account of the Process

The China Child Welfare Association promotes Children's Day to the fathers and elders of the nation. The fathers and elders of the nation, the parents of children across the country, promote Children's Day and seek to open up sources of happiness for children across the country. The Child Welfare Association will take the lead in advocating Children's Day in China. It must inform the fathers and elders of the nation, the parents of children across the country. However, what we want to tell you is not to make the fathers and elders suddenly recognize Children's Day, but to first recognize the children themselves. It is also not to ask the fathers and elders to immediately promote Children's Day, but to first raise the status of children. Only in this way can we move from recognizing Children's Day to promoting Children's Day. We will use the following points to analyze these two perspectives: (1) Children with parents should no longer be regarded as the private property of their parents. Parents who regard children as their private property believe that children are born and raised by me, are my flesh and blood, my things that no one else can interfere with or have a share in. Since they belong to me, I have full power to control their life and death, their joys and sorrows, to do as I please, and no one dares to disobey. If there is any violation, they will be denounced as unfilial, evil, beasts, snakes, or scorpions, and either publicly sent to law or privately expelled. Such facts and news can still be seen and heard in the newspapers here. They do not know that children are the children of society and the nation, not the private property of the parents who give birth to and raise them. And the nurture and cultivation of parents is also their obligation to their children and their responsibility to the country. Therefore, those who previously regarded the achievement of their children as bringing glory to their ancestors must now change to regarding the achievement of their children as strengthening the country and benefiting the people. Those who previously regarded children as inheriting their parents' business and family must now regard children as workers who bear social responsibilities and leaders who take on national affairs. If we can change from that kind of erroneous concept to this clear understanding, it is not only recognizing children but also recognizing Children's Day. (2) Children without parents should no longer be regarded as social tumors. Children who are social tumors are abandoned on the roadside and left in the wilderness because they have no father or no mother or no parents at all. If they are fortunate enough to be glimpsed by compassionate and benevolent people, they will either be taken in or kept and raised. Although their intentions are very good, they always think that there are not many of these children, and it is not a loss to get rid of them. They only think about saving their lives, doing good deeds, and accumulating virtue for their descendants. Therefore, these children are regarded as social tumors. Those who see them call them "orphans" and "wretched children." Orphans and wretched children have become a special class, ostracized by the people and unwelcome by the country. Such popular concepts and measures can be seen clearly like a movie with just a glance and a thought. They do not know that all children, whether with or without parents, are children of the nation and children of society. Those with parents must be responsible for education and upbringing on behalf of the country, while those without parents must naturally have the responsibility for education and upbringing borne by the national government or the public parents of society. They must not be despised as social tumors or national parasites because they have no parents. If members of society take the public parents of these children without parents as their responsibility, and the national government can also do so, then what is the difference between these children without parents and those with parents? What is the difference between their future achievements and those of children with parents? If the fathers and elders can recognize themselves as the public parents of children without parents, then they can also proceed to recognize Children's Day. (3) The benefits of family and society should no longer be grown into the patent of adults. When we open our eyes and look around, we can see everywhere that the current equipment in families and the arrangements in society are all for the enjoyment of adults, and very few are planned for children. On average, there is one child in every family of four or more people, so children account for a quarter of the social population. Moreover, in terms of family, children spend more time in the family than adults who go out early and return late. In terms of society, children have more leisure time than adults. It is only right that more toys, books, and supplies should be provided for children in families so that children can take advantage of the longer time spent in the family to self-educate. In society, more parks, playgrounds, libraries, and schools should also be arranged for children so that children can take advantage of the more free time in society.

The Ultimate Fate of Tuberculosis Bacteria (Translated from a German Journal on Pulmonary Tuberculosis) 121

The Pathogenic Bacteria of Pulmonary Tuberculosis

Since Dr. Robert Koch of Germany announced the discovery of the tuberculosis bacterium as the pathogen of pulmonary tuberculosis, medical professionals have generally been able to transplant purely cultured tuberculosis bacteria into guinea pigs, causing them to develop the same tuberculosis. Tuberculosis bacteria can be cultured in bouillon-based agar and coagulated blood serum containing glycerol. However, their development is quite selective and completely different from that of other bacteria. The shape of tuberculosis bacteria is similar to that of a rod. They are non-motile and extremely small. They may be straight or curved. They can only be seen with the naked eye when thousands of them are gathered in one place. To cover the small area of a postage stamp, 16 million tuberculosis bacteria are required. As for their method of reproduction, it is based on their own fission process, dividing from one into two, two into four, and four into eight, gradually doubling. Therefore, the rate of reproduction is extremely alarming. If allowed to reproduce in a suitable environment, a single bacterium will multiply into millions in a single day. These bacteria often cluster in the sputum of tuberculosis patients. According to Dr. Haelre, one lump of sputum from a tuberculosis patient contains more than 300 million tuberculosis bacteria. If the patient expectorates sputum once every hour, then 7.2 billion tuberculosis bacteria will be discharged from the patient's lungs and spread into the air throughout the day. People are attacked by them morning and evening. However, the patient does not reduce their number by discharging them because tuberculosis bacteria, as mentioned above, divide and reproduce without stopping, and their power gradually increases. Now, let us assume that their rate of increase is one fission process every hour. Then, in 24 hours, one tuberculosis bacterium will suddenly transform into more than 16 million. Is this not frightening?

The Resistance of Tuberculosis Bacteria 122

The reproductive power of tuberculosis bacteria is alarming, as mentioned above. But their resistance is even more terrifying. If the sputum of a tuberculosis patient is exposed to the air, the tuberculosis bacteria can survive for more than half a year. If placed in a dark room, they can still survive for more than a year. However, tuberculosis bacteria cannot reproduce very well outside the human or animal body and have little resistance to sunlight. They are easily killed if directly exposed to strong light. This is because the temperature has a great influence on these bacteria. They generally die in six hours at a temperature of 50 degrees Celsius, die in one hour at 60 degrees, and die in two minutes at 90 degrees. In addition to temperature, their resistance to many chemical drugs is surprisingly high. They do not die even after 24 hours in a mercury chloride solution with a concentration of 0.2%. If 5% carbolic acid solution is added and stirred once, or if pure alcohol is added to the sputum in about ten times the amount, they will die only after 24 hours.

It is well known that tuberculosis is a chronic disease that is difficult to cure. There is no need to elaborate. This is because tuberculosis bacteria can secrete an acid-resistant waxy substance from their own bodies, which encapsulates the bacterial body as a protective armor. Therefore, they are most resistant to general chemical drugs. In addition, the part that stimulates their attachment and reproduction forms extremely strong nodules, so that all bactericidal drugs cannot reach their bacterial bodies. Alas, the greatest difficulty for doctors in the East and West in researching tuberculosis bactericides has always been this point. The bactericides and disinfectants that we call today are all protoplasmic toxins, and what can kill bacteria can also destroy the cells and tissues of the body. Therefore, the ideal therapeutic agent for tuberculosis that the medical community hopes for today must have the following prerequisites:

(1) Any drug that can penetrate into the tuberculous body and can directly act on tuberculosis bacteria.

(2) It can also strip and dissolve the acid-resistant waxy membrane LIPOD of tuberculosis bacteria.

(3) It can completely kill tuberculosis bacteria without harming the human body.

Diagram of Pulmonary Lymph Node Arrangement (Made by Dr. Kangnigao, a Great Pulmonary Doctor)

New Medical Technique for Devaxing and Destroying Tuberculosis Bacteria 123

The cause of pulmonary tuberculosis (i.e., tuberculosis) is tuberculosis bacteria. When this bacterium enters the human body, it forms a nodule at that location, blocking the path of blood circulation. In addition, tuberculosis bacteria can secrete an acid-resistant waxy substance, which surrounds their bodies to prevent the invasion of all external drug forces. Therefore, although various bactericidal drugs are taken internally or injected, they cannot reach the substance of the bacteria. The natural therapy, symptomatic therapy, physical therapy, serum therapy, drug therapy, and all other therapies that doctors have always used have not been completely successful. And the saying that there is no medicine for tuberculosis is prevalent in the world because they do not know this profound theory. Therefore, modern tuberculosis scholars have continued to study based on the above-mentioned theory without sparing any effort. As a result, this chemical holy drug that can kill all tuberculosis bacteria has been developed, called Sanosin. This drug was successfully developed in accordance with the latest medical theories of Dr. Robert Koch of Germany, the discoverer of tuberculosis bacteria, and Dr. De or Bergier, the inventor of tuberculosis bacteria devaxing technology. According to the current experimental reports of various tuberculosis sanatoriums in Germany, Switzerland, and other countries, this drug has the effect of penetrating the nodules of pulmonary tuberculosis foci and dissolving waxy substances. It also has bactericidal power and can radically cure first, second, and third stage tuberculosis. It is indeed a special medicine with ten thousand tests and ten thousand spirits. In China, the National Government Central Health Experimental Institute has tested it. The medicinal properties are mild and non-toxic, and there are no side effects whatsoever. The following briefly describes the therapeutic effects:

(1) If the medicinal power of (Sanosin) is tested in a test tube, the acid resistance of tuberculosis bacteria will disappear after one minute. After three minutes, the tuberculosis bacteria will be completely killed, with none spared.

(2) According to animal experiments, it was found that (Sanosin) can penetrate into the tuberculosis foci. If the latent tuberculosis bacteria in the foci are examined, they all lose their acid resistance. This proves that the waxy substance has been completely dissolved.

(3) If the patient takes (Sanosin) internally for about a week, a good condition such as thinning of expectoration and lowering of body temperature will be seen immediately.

(4) If (Sanosin) is continued to be taken internally for more than thirty to sixty days, a significant increase in body weight and appetite will be seen, and all symptoms will gradually ease, eventually achieving the great feat of returning to life.

Conflict Between Tram Ticket Inspector and Shipyard Craftsmen 128

Mayor Zhang Appointed to Mediate

The details of the conflict between Zhou Xiaoliu and Lin Honghai, craftsmen at the Jiangnan Shipyard of the Ministry of Navy, and a ticket inspector from the China Merchants Tram Company, were reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that Mayor Zhang Yuejun has been appointed to mediate. The details are recorded as follows:

Mayor's Appointment to Mediate: After the incident occurred the day before yesterday, Director Chen Shaokuan of the Jiangnan Shipyard happened to be in Shanghai. He ordered the commander of the guard battalion, Ye Binqi, to go to the tram company and request that the manager of the tram company, Lu Bohong, come to the shipyard within an hour to discuss a solution. After Mayor Zhang heard about this, fearing the matter would escalate, he immediately contacted Chen by telephone, saying that he would be responsible for mediating everything. Chen expressed his agreement to Mayor Zhang's appointment to mediate and dispatched Wang Shouting, captain of the Hai Rong warship, and Li Mengbin, captain of the Hai Chou warship, to be responsible for discussing the incident with Mayor Zhang. It is hoped that a satisfactory solution can be reached in the shortest possible time. That evening, Chen took a train back to Beijing.

Company's Perspective: Lu Bohong, the general manager of the company, went to the municipal government at 10:00 AM yesterday to meet with Mayor Zhang. After reporting the details of the incident, Mayor Zhang met with him and mediated the case between the two parties, seeking a fair and peaceful solution. The company's previous request to the Public Utilities Bureau, the Social Affairs Bureau, and the Public Security Bureau to mediate the case of temporarily maintaining the issuance of tram passes to the Jiangnan Shipyard of the Ordnance Factory in 1927, with the factory subsidizing the company for the pass fees on a monthly basis, had not been resolved. As a result, conflicts have occurred from time to time between the tram workers and the factory workers. Therefore, it is hoped that the tram passes can be resolved through various methods during this period to avoid future incidents. It is said that this matter will likely be resolved together.

Workers' Perspective: Yesterday, the Jiangnan Shipyard Labor Union and the Shanghai South Water and Electricity Labor Union issued separate declarations, each holding its own position. Subsequently, due to the mediation of Lu Bohong, the general manager of the company, and the higher-level authorities, Mayor Zhang and Vice Minister Chen, it is expected that the matter will be handled fairly. Therefore, the workers on both sides are waiting quietly for the authorities to handle it. There were no other actions yesterday, and they continued to work as usual.

Various News from Both Sides: Yesterday morning, Chen contacted the shipyard from Beijing by long-distance telephone, ordering the craftsmen to work calmly and quietly on the one hand, and instructing the section to draft a letter (recorded later) to Mayor Zhang Qun, requesting the punishment of the instigator on the other hand. However, the Jiangnan Shipyard Labor Union issued a declaration yesterday (omitted) and a public statement (omitted). Their anger was still unable to dissipate for a while. The China Merchants Tram Company also submitted the blurred pass No. ○661 of Zhou Xiaoliu, along with the report of the inspector and ticket seller and the injury certificate from the Shanghai Hospital, to the authorities for handling. The letter from Chen Shaokuan, Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard, to Shanghai Mayor Zhang Qun, and the Labor Union's proclamation are recorded below:

Letter from Director Chen: Respectfully, at 12:50 PM on the 3rd of this month, Zhou Xiaoliu, a worker from our shipyard, was on the No. 4 tram of the China Merchants Tram Company. The ticket seller No. 12 inspected his tram pass and claimed that the photo was blurred. The ticket seller forcibly confiscated the pass and forcibly removed the badge given to Zhou Xiaoliu by our shipyard. Zhou argued, and when the tram arrived in front of the tram company, the ticket seller gathered a crowd to beat Zhou and tried to drag him into the company. Lin Honghai, a worker from our shipyard, stepped forward to mediate but was instead resented and handed over to the police. At that time, all the workers in our shipyard received the news. Angered by the repeated arrests, beatings, and insults by the tram company, they immediately went on strike and were about to go to the company to argue. For the sake of local stability, our shipyard agreed to take responsibility for handling the matter and persuaded them to wait quietly for a resolution. The workers' tram passes have been used for a long time, and our shipyard has repeatedly sent letters urging for replacements, but the company has always delayed and eventually ignored them. In fact, they intentionally made the passes blurred in order to gradually confiscate and destroy them, allowing their ticket inspectors and ticket sellers to pick on people in various ways, causing disputes, blaming the workers, and fabricating false statements to deceive the public. This time, they even dared to remove our shipyard's badge without authorization and arrest our shipyard's craftsmen. This is an extreme insult to our shipyard. To trace the origin of the disaster, it is imperative to severely punish the manager of the company. Accordingly, I am writing to request that your municipal government order the arrest and punishment of the manager of the company to punish the instigator and appease public anger. As for the losses suffered by our shipyard due to the company's incitement of trouble and causing a strike, they should also be ordered to compensate. I would appreciate it if you could inform us of how to handle this matter. Respectfully, [signed] Chen, Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard, to Zhang, Mayor of Shanghai Special Municipality.

Shipyard Labor Union's Proclamation: For the matter of the proclamation: Regarding the dispute between the workers of the China Merchants Tram Company and members of our union yesterday, the facts have been reported and filed. We have received instructions to have the director take responsibility for handling the matter, and all craftsmen should work calmly and wait for a resolution, etc. Therefore, we hereby issue this proclamation for your information.

Yesterday (the 4th) was the second day of the 12th Annual Meeting of the Chinese Medical and Pharmaceutical Association. Members reported on their experiences, including (1) Yao Yongzheng's research on malaria in the capital, (2) Lai Douyan's comparison of diphtheria prevention methods, (3) Liu Qijing's five cases of liver abscess surgery, and (4) Liu Yaoxi's research on the basilar artery of the human brain in China. The meeting finally concluded at 5:30 PM. After the meeting, everyone went to visit the Central and Shanghai Hygiene Testing Institute. In the evening, they attended a public banquet at the East Asia Restaurant at the invitation of the Three Students' Association. At 8:00 PM, a popular lecture was held, with Hu Ding'an, Sheng Peicong, Pang Jingzhou, Zhao Wuqiao, and others as speakers. The meeting adjourned at 10:00 PM. The meeting will continue today, and a popular hygiene lecture will be held in the evening, with Chen Zhuoren and Ding Rensheng taking on the responsibilities. Executive Yuan Approves Special Business Tax on Foil Products 130

Allocates 570,000 Yuan for Educational Expenses

Partially Allocated to Prepare for the Livelihood of Foil Workers

The Foil Industry Association previously asked the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to send a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, urging it to correct the business tax on foil products in Zhejiang Province in order to reduce the burden on merchants. It is now known that the Ministry of Finance has telegraphed back to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, saying that it previously received the association's telegram requesting the cancellation of the business tax on foil products in Zhejiang and the return of the taxes already collected. The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance reported that this foil tax was previously decided by the Provincial Government Committee to be changed to a special business tax on foil products, which will continue to be collected according to the old regulations. The Zhejiang Provincial Government also reported to the ministry for review. Subsequently, the Executive Yuan issued Instruction No. 390, stating that the foil tax is unique to Zhejiang Province and that the revenue has been designated for educational expenses and Zhejiang provincial expenses, which will continue to be handled by Zhejiang Province as originally approved. Furthermore, the Provincial Government Committee agreed that foil products are entirely superstitious items and were previously ordered by the central government to be banned. The former provincial government presented a request for temporary postponement of the implementation due to the livelihood of hundreds of thousands of foil workers and stated that this type of business should be treated with the intention of prohibiting it through taxation and cannot be compared with other ordinary businesses. In addition, the majority of these foil products are sold in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, so it is named the Special Business Tax on Foil Products in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces. From the former special tax on foil products, 300,000 yuan per year was originally allocated to the central educational expenses, and 270,000 yuan per year to Jiangsu Province, which will continue to be allocated by Zhejiang Province as originally approved. In addition, a portion will be allocated to prepare for the livelihood of foil workers. The Jiangsu Department of Finance was also consulted, stating that foil products from Zhejiang sold in Jiangsu Province will no longer be subject to other taxes to avoid double taxation and comply with the spirit of the Executive Yuan's order to handle the matter as originally approved. The ministry has already issued instructions in addition to notifying you by telegram. [signed] Ministry of Finance.

Business Tax Certificates for Various Industries Should Be Applied for with the Seal of the Trade Association 131

Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Negotiate with the Financial Authorities

The Tax Regulations Research Committee of the Shanghai Municipal Trade Associations sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday regarding the issuance of business tax certificates, requesting negotiation for the application with the seal of each industry association. The letter stated: Respectfully, we have examined Article 10 of the revised Zhejiang Provincial Business Tax Regulations by the Ministry of Finance, which states that the calculation of the business tax amount is based on the industry. If a household engages in several businesses with different tax rates, it should be determined according to the main part of its business. Article 12 of the same regulations states that businesses should report the following items to the collecting agency within one month after the promulgation of these regulations and within the last month of each year thereafter to apply for a business certificate. The regulations stipulate that newly established businesses should report before starting their business. In terms of its meaning, the collection of business tax is based on the industry, and applying for a business certificate is the first step before starting business or collecting taxes. In the future, when Shanghai launches business tax, it should follow the same procedure. However, Shanghai's commercial market is prosperous, and the division of industries is very strict. Some industries are similar in form but different in reality, and some are the same in reality but operate in different ways. As for what is the main part, it cannot be distinguished by those who do not understand the situation in the industry. However, the organization of the industry association is based on the industry. Examining the laws and regulations of the industrial and commercial associations and observing the situation of each industry association, one can understand without a doubt that the issuance of a business certificate can be filled out by the operator and handed over to the affiliated industry association for sealing and certification. If it has not been sealed and certified by the industry association, it will not be issued. This will prevent confusion in the collecting agency and provide convenience for taxpayers. It is a win-win situation. It is hereby resolved by the ninth committee meeting of our association to transfer the request to your association to negotiate with the municipal financial authorities to ensure that the seal is issued, and a case is recorded accordingly and sent to the association for your review and handling. Sincerely, [signed].
